  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_783713a5-060d-4ca3-bdde-d783e440bf4d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer10949638108542124964">When Lauren Monroe first laid eyes on Michael Delaney back in high school, she had every reason to stay away from him; within minutes of their first encounter, his volatile actions confirmed his notorious reputation.   <span id="freeText10949638108542124964" style="display:none">When Lauren Monroe first laid eyes on Michael Delaney back in high school, she had every reason to stay away from him; within minutes of their first encounter, his volatile actions confirmed his notorious reputation. But Lauren saw something in him that caused her to question his bad-boy persona, and against her better judgment, she took a chance. She had no way of knowing that the unlikely friendship they formed would become so important to her.<br /><br />Or that it would end so painfully.<br /><br />Eight years later, when Lauren begins her new job at Learn and Grow Day Care, Michael is the last person she expects to see. Refusing to revisit the hurt and confusion of their past, Lauren vows to keep her distance from him. But staying away from Michael proves to be more difficult than she thought, despite her lingering grief and her instincts for self-preservation.<br /><br />As Lauren and Michael recall the friendship that changed them forever and the events that tore them apart, will they finally be able to heal? Or will the ghosts of Michael’s past prove to be too much to overcome?</span>

<div id="review_447724756" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/447724756" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/447724756?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer447724756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13306289339745599994"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764041.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Oh my God. Oh my God. <u> OH</u>. <u> MY</u>. <u> GOD</u>. </b><br/><br/>Guys, you all HAVE to read this book!<br/><br/><i> <b> “Right back to him. Always to him.” </b></i> <br/><br/>Its a beautiful, believable second-chance friends-to-lovers story that was both heart breaking and heart warming, with an uplifting, satisfying ending that left me clutching my heart, with happy tears in my eyes and a smile on my face :)<br/><br/>I loved it.<br/><br/>I started this book late last night after a long day at work and it kept me glued to my kindle until I finished it at 3:30AM. I couldn’t </span>
  <span id="freeText13306289339745599994" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764041.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Oh my God. Oh my God. <u> OH</u>. <u> MY</u>. <u> GOD</u>. </b><br><br>Guys, you all HAVE to read this book!<br><br><i> <b> “Right back to him. Always to him.” </b></i> <br><br>Its a beautiful, believable second-chance friends-to-lovers story that was both heart breaking and heart warming, with an uplifting, satisfying ending that left me clutching my heart, with happy tears in my eyes and a smile on my face :)<br><br>I loved it.<br><br>I started this book late last night after a long day at work and it kept me glued to my kindle until I finished it at 3:30AM. I couldn’t put it down!! My heart was just SO wrapped up in the story and so connected to the characters!<br><br>This is the unlikely-friends-to-lovers story about Michael Delaney, an angry badass badboy with a tragic past, and Lauren Monroe, the straight-lace good girl who saw through his facade and into his heart.<br><br><i> “His face, like everything she knew about him, was purely contradictory… He was too lovely to be menacing, but too intense to be innocent.” </i><br><br>Eight years ago, when they were still in high school, was when Lauren first saw Michael. Everyone treated him as though he was dangerous, with a constant stream of angry, violent outbursts, a string a suspensions, and an all-round rebellious attitude, people were afraid of him. But something about his demeanor called to Lauren. She was inexplicably drawn to him, seeing something in him that no one else did. They became best friends throughout the rest of school until something happened that tore them apart leaving her heart bruised without answers.<br><br>Now, eight years later, Lauren has just started a new job teaching a kindergarten class and the last person she expects to see is Michael. The rush of emotions and memories that flood back when she sees him shows that there is still something deep between them, but Michael needs to win back her trust, and Lauren needs answers as to what tore them apart. And together they find that no amount of separation can change the depth of their feelings for each other.<br><br><i> <b> “It suddenly felt like there was a magnet in her chest, like some unforeseen force was pulling her toward him.” </b></i> <br><br>The smoothly flowing writing style beautifully depicts the depth of the story. The author perfectly captured the emotions of her characters and projects them onto you. You feel them as though they were yours.<br><br>The story is told in a mixture of past and present day story lines. Starting out with the present and intermingling it with bits of where Lauren and Michael’s story began 8 years ago. There are alternating POVs with an initial focus on Lauren’s but with just enough of Michael’s to keep us strongly connected to him on a more personal level.<br><br>This book spoke to my heart. You know the kind of story where, if it says, <i> “Michael grinned” </i>, it makes your heart feel full? Yeah, its that kind of book <br><br>I literally would just read scene after scene with my hand over my heart either smiling or near tears. Parts were sweet, parts gave me shivers, parts broke my heart and parts put it back together so beautifully that I forgot everything but the happiness.<br><br>I loved that it was a much deeper friends-to-lovers story than the usual… they were friends but with something so much deeper than that – a connection that that kept drawing them together in every way.<br><br><i> <b> “I always knew I would fall in love with you,” he said softly, “But you were never supposed to love me back.” </b></i> <br><br>Lauren was a wonderful heroine. She was a straight up, no-stupidity, honest, kind, intelligent and deeply understanding character who made me totally sympathetic to everything she went though.<br><br>And Michael, I fell in love with right from the start of the story. Like Lauren, I felt drawn to him. The mystery, his pain, the kind heart that was hidden behind the layers of hurt just melted me &lt;3<br><br>I love these second-chance stories where the characters get a chance to make things right again by finding a way to build new, positive memories over the painful ones and find a way to heal and build a beautiful life together.<br><br><i> <b> “…I never stopped loving you. Not for one second.” </b></i> <br><br>I was so emotional for the last 20% of the book. You know that constantly-near-tears, brimming-with-emotion feeling? I had that! So much heart-break, heart warming, and healing, with an achingly beautiful love scene and a wonderful epilogue.<br><br>I love stories that have some heart ache in them as well as happiness because sometimes, its through the pain that you can come to appreciate more fully the beauty that life and love have to offer. Not that it is necessarily needed to appreciate it, but those who have gone through it know how lucky they are to have that love. Michael and Lauren knew it. It was absolutely beautiful!<br><br>Its got a bit of both a YA story (their past) and an adult story (their present). There is steam, but its more emotionally descriptive than blatantly graphic.<br><br>Fans of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2730715.Al_Jackson" title="Al Jackson" rel="nofollow noopener">Al Jackson</a>’s books will definitely love this.<br><br>**little note because I know some of you will be wondering about this: there is no cheating in this book. There is a whiff of a love triangle at one point, but it doesn’t go anywhere or get developed into a source of angst so your hearts can rest easy.<br><br>I am utterly floored that this is a debut novel. I won’t be surprised if this book makes it onto best-seller lists. It was released recently but I just know that once people catch on and start reading it, its going to be huge!<br><br>Everyone should add it to their to-read lists :)<br><br><i> Thank you to the author for offering to send me a copy to review! </i><br><br>CASTING for Michael and Lauren (see above as well):<br><br><img width="80%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764042._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="80%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764043.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13306289339745599994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/453904085" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/453904085?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453904085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer635742644142828585"><b>Where in the hell did this book come from and where can I get some more...</b><br/><br/>This is one of those reviews where I don't even know where to start. Reviewing, with words, a book that has rendered you speechless can be quite challenging. It was so well written it hurt. Priscilla Glenn has debuted and she has debuted hard!<br/><br/>This book is pure genius. You get to fall in love with Michael and Lauren twice! You <i>will</i> fall in love with Michael and Lauren. You experience a hurricane of emotions during a passion</span>
  <span id="freeText635742644142828585" style="display:none"><b>Where in the hell did this book come from and where can I get some more...</b><br /><br />This is one of those reviews where I don't even know where to start. Reviewing, with words, a book that has rendered you speechless can be quite challenging. It was so well written it hurt. Priscilla Glenn has debuted and she has debuted hard!<br /><br />This book is pure genius. You get to fall in love with Michael and Lauren twice! You <i>will</i> fall in love with Michael and Lauren. You experience a hurricane of emotions during a passionate storm of the past and present. It's a YA-fiction and adult contemporary love child! It's like the author took a list of all of my favorite things and put them into one book! It was developed in a way that drew me in, grabbed my heart, and didn't let go. Even after the book ended...it didn't let go.<br /><br />This book contains one of the best love scenes I've ever read...EVER! Not because of "this" being touched or "that" being clamped. Not because of the "Oh Gods" or multiples. I'm not even saying it was the "hottest" scene I've ever read, but it left me breathless. I couldn't breathe over the passion and intimacy of that one moment. A moment that I wanted to make love to and carry with me forever. It was innocent. It was real. It was something I experienced right along with them. <br /><br />I honestly don't know what it was about this book, but it captured me from the start. It was everything I needed in a book and more. It was heart wrenching, heart breaking, heart healing, and even funny...<br /><br /> <b>"See, Red? When life hands you lemons, you know what you gotta do now."<br /> "Yes, Mr. Cliche, I know what I have to do. I make lemonade."<br /> "No," he said. "You scream, <i>'Fuck you, lemons!"'</i></b><br /><br />Like it, love it, read it, hate it. I really don't care because I felt like this book was written just for me. It pulled me right into the pulse of the story and became mine! I honestly wish I was White Oprah and could gift you all a copy, but I can't so...READ ON!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="635742644142828585" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer446183900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3454337181831896847">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/?m=1' rel='nofollow noopener'> Swept Away By Romance</a> <br/><br/><b>3 to 31/2 stars</b> <br/><br/><i>Back To You</i> is a sweet, well written, slightly angsty, and engaging romance about second chances. The story is told in present day and flashback segments, giving the reader a thoroughly comprehensive and engaging look into Michael and Lauren's current and past relationship. This couple develops a close friendship during their high school years, but it ends badly and they go their separate ways. Fast forward eight years and they are unexpec</span>
  <span id="freeText3454337181831896847" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/?m=1" rel="nofollow noopener"> Swept Away By Romance</a> <br /><br /><b>3 to 31/2 stars</b> <br /><br /><i>Back To You</i> is a sweet, well written, slightly angsty, and engaging romance about second chances. The story is told in present day and flashback segments, giving the reader a thoroughly comprehensive and engaging look into Michael and Lauren's current and past relationship. This couple develops a close friendship during their high school years, but it ends badly and they go their separate ways. Fast forward eight years and they are unexpectedly reunited again. This plot isn't particularly original but the execution felt refreshing. <br /><br />What I enjoyed the most about this book was the flashback segments of the story. I felt the relationship between Michael and Lauren during their high school years had an authentic feel that resonated with me. Although I was somewhat ambivalent about the hero, I found this couple's interactions endearing and captivating. <br /><br />My problem with the book–<b>other than falling head-over-heels in love with the secondary love interest, Adam</b>–was that Michael, the hero, never fully convinced me that his feelings for the heroine ran deeper than friendship. Although I smiled at the feel-good ending, this couple's romance never fully clicked for me. <br /><br />As for the heroine, while I found her endearing as a teenager, I had a hard time relating to her as an adult. At times her behavior aggravated me. If I'm being honest with myself, however, that probably had more to do with the fact that I was rooting for Lauren and Adam and not Lauren and Michael (the hero). In addition, Lauren's treatment of Adam before she ended their relationship was less than admirable and made it clear to me that she wasn't good enough for him. Okay...I'm sure it's a little obvious I'm <i>still</i> a bit miffed that Adam didn't get his HEA. Lol. <br /><br />Overall, I liked this book and have no doubt readers who love charming second-chance-at-romance plotlines will enjoy this story. <br /><br /><br /><i>Arc provided by author</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11583779577831537944"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390503865i/8233534._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397478i/767013._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I love those stories where the unlikely pair become friends and then inevitably fall in love and Back To You was no exception. This was a really beautiful story.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>And she couldn't help but smile at the irony of the fact that the baddest boy in school could somehow always make her feel like the world was good.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I loved the flashbacks. Soooo adorable! Think Dirty Dancing, plate smashing, spontaneous make-outs and a pizza dates. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“The crust is the best part,” he explained around his mouthful of f</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11583779577831537944" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390503865i/8233534._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397478i/767013._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love those stories where the unlikely pair become friends and then inevitably fall in love and Back To You was no exception. This was a really beautiful story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>And she couldn't help but smile at the irony of the fact that the baddest boy in school could somehow always make her feel like the world was good.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved the flashbacks. Soooo adorable! Think Dirty Dancing, plate smashing, spontaneous make-outs and a pizza dates. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The crust is the best part,” he explained around his mouthful of food. “If they made an all-crust pizza, I’d be a pig in shit.”<br>Lauren took a delicate bite of her own slice. “I’m pretty sure they do. It’s called bread.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>But despite the light hearted majority of this book, it all contends with some very dark issues. Some of the flashbacks to Michael's childhood were truly heartbreaking. I found myself sniffling back the tears on a couple of occasions.<br><br>Lauren was a likeable heroine. I loved her relationship with Erin, Michael's three year old daughter, too. She was loving, understanding, kind hearted but strong too. Her thought processes made sense and I liked that she wasn't hell bent on making Michael's life a misery because of the pain he'd put her through.<br><br>And then there's Michael... who doesn't love a high school badass turned doting Daddy?!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397478i/767014.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Completely adorable. The story of how he came to have full custody of Erin is precious. And, with his determination to have Lauren back in his life, it's impossible not to fall in love with him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I always knew I would fall in love with you, but you were never supposed to love me back."<br>"What did you just say?"<br>"I loved you. So much. My God, more than anything."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Squeeeee! Super duper cute! And the epilogue is just... *does happy dance* gorgeous. A definite must read!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397478i/767015._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=cringeworthy">cringeworthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=2015-read">2015-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=slut-shaming">slut-shaming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=roll-eyes-worthy">roll-eyes-worthy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1266172262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16707459551552174752"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430161934i/14687847._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>This review had disappeared this morning. WTF?! Fortunately I had it on my computer. <i>Sigh</i>.</b><br/><br/>For all my adorable friends who asked me how was my first day after vacations : It was exhausting. <i>Sigh</i>. Now, the fact that I didn't sleep at all yesterday might explain this. <i>Sigh repetita</i>. <br/><br/><b>Results</b> : I'm exhausted, disappointed, and felt hollow in the end, because I was expecting so much more from this book! Therefore excuse me if I keep it short, but I'm going to write an old-school <i>I like/I didn't like/I</i></span>
  <span id="freeText16707459551552174752" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430161934i/14687847._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>This review had disappeared this morning. WTF?! Fortunately I had it on my computer. <i>Sigh</i>.</b><br><br>For all my adorable friends who asked me how was my first day after vacations : It was exhausting. <i>Sigh</i>. Now, the fact that I didn't sleep at all yesterday might explain this. <i>Sigh repetita</i>. <br><br><b>Results</b> : I'm exhausted, disappointed, and felt hollow in the end, because I was expecting so much more from this book! Therefore excuse me if I keep it short, but I'm going to write an old-school <i>I like/I didn't like/I hated</i> review. Because <i>I'm such a lazy lady today</i>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430161934i/14687848._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<i>Blablabla</i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16111679-back-to-you?ac=1" rel="nofollow noopener"> the <b>plot</b></a>]<br><br>▒ <b>What I liked</b> ▒<br><br>▨ <b>Erin</b>. Indeed when it's well-done I usually love when children get involved in a story and as it was the case here it was no exception : her stubbornness made me laugh, and as a former teacher of Kindergarten, I found her voice believable and refreshing. <br><br>▨ <b>The flashbacks during Michael's childhood</b>. Don't get fooled, these passages made me RAGE because how can we abandon a child that way? Oh, God. To see him so lonely and lost broke my heart. Literally. I'm going to write it : I HATE HIS PARENTS. WHAT FUCKING ASSHOLES. BOTH OF THEM. Okay, now that it's in the out, I must admit that these flashbacks were the only moments of the book where I <i>felt</i> something, so I count them in my likes. <br><br>▒ <b>What I didn't like that much</b> ▒<br><br>▨ <b>Lauren and Michael relationship</b>. Why? Because she's basically a special snowflake who is <i>pure</i> and <i>better</i> than every single one of the other girls and I didn't buy their romance one second in present days. I felt NO. CHEMISTRY. At all. Nope. Frankly, I didn't hate them as a couple but I just didn't care much. Moreover, I never felt their relationship growing - I mean, the guys don't talk for 8 YEARS and to me the only talk they have about the past isn't enough, by far, to explain the resolution. <br><br>▨ <b>The boredom</b>. You know the kind of books where you keep turning the pages <s>clicking on your reader</s> and that you finish without even realizing it? <b>Well, that wasn't that. Fuck no</b>. That was the exact opposite. <br><br>▒ <b>What I hated</b> ▒<br><br>▨ <b>Michael's character</b>, in the teenage times. Now, I just <b>hate violent behavior, hey, that's me.</b> WAIT - Hmm OF COURSE I HATE VIOLENT BEHAVIOR. I don't find it sexy, nope nope nope, and even if his violence never aimed at Lauren, I don't find it okay. To be fair, the kid had serious shit going on and I didn't feel like the author was saying that it was okay. But I really, really have a hard time with Lauren's <s>reactions</s> absence of reaction. <br><br>▨ <b>Slut-shaming </b>. Oh. My. God. I thought I'd throw my Kindle at some point, because Lauren just can't SHUT THE HELL UP and keeps referring to the girls Michael dated - or slept with, for that matter - as sluts, whores, and even <i>"worthless girls"</i>. <b>OH, FUCK YOU, LAUREN. JUST FUCK YOU</b>. <br><br><i>Voilà!</i> <b>It was my lazy review</b>. Sorry about that. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430161934i/14687849._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>PS : I feel so unfair towards my cats right now. I know, you're not ALWAYS lazy. Let's say, most of the time, okay?<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_454527059" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454527059" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454527059?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781479103782" href="/book/show/16114910-back-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=second-chance-romance">second-chance-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=6-shining-stars">6-shining-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454527059" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4331339195026233995"><b>OMG, LOVE, LOVE LOVE!!! THIS BOOK IS ABSOLUTE PERFECTION! </b><br/><br/>Every now and then a little indie book pops up that is a total surprise and just completely takes your breath away. This is that book. An absolutely beautifully written love story that made me laugh, cry, and squee over and over. I was gripped from the first page and couldn’t put it down.<br/><br/>It tells the story of Lauren and Michael, who are unexpectedly reunited after not seeing each other for eight years. When they first see each other in th</span>
  <span id="freeText4331339195026233995" style="display:none"><b>OMG, LOVE, LOVE LOVE!!! THIS BOOK IS ABSOLUTE PERFECTION! </b><br /><br />Every now and then a little indie book pops up that is a total surprise and just completely takes your breath away. This is that book. An absolutely beautifully written love story that made me laugh, cry, and squee over and over. I was gripped from the first page and couldn’t put it down.<br /><br />It tells the story of Lauren and Michael, who are unexpectedly reunited after not seeing each other for eight years. When they first see each other in the book, there is an obvious intensity between them, and from that point the book splits into dual POVs and starts to jump around in time as the story of their past is interwoven with the story of their present. <br /><br />Good girl Lauren befriended Michael in high school. It’s a relationship that nobody else understands as pretty much everybody else in school is afraid of the volatile bad boy, but Lauren sees past that to the real Michael, and as they get to know each other, they discover that they have something very special together. Very quickly they become the best of friends, and the unfolding of their story is absolutely sensational as they are there for each other absolutely and completely. There are some really emotionally intense moments as the story delves further back into Michael’s horrific past, and we see how the traumatic events that he went through as a child impacted on his life. But I also laughed a lot and had a grin on my face pretty much the entire time I was reading about them in high school. A romance begins to emerge as Lauren falls in love with Michael but, despite how he feels, he thinks that she’s too good for him and is not prepared to risk what they have together to do anything further. It all builds up to a mysterious ‘incident’ where Michael does something that tears Lauren’s world apart and they lose contact. <br /><br />Watching them reconnect as adults with all of the murky history between them is intense as the two of them battle with their feelings over everything that happened when they were younger, as well as understanding how those events shaped who they became as adults, and what that means for them now. <br /><br />The pacing is perfect as Lauren and Michael reconnect and an incredibly intimate, honest and passionate love story unfolds. You feel the strong emotional connection between them from the very beginning, but there is so much that they both have to work through in figuring out what they are feeling. It’s a slow build, but watching Lauren and Michael find their way back to each other is so worth the wait because when it happens… O.M.G!! I was in floods of tears. Yes… floods!<br /><br /><i>“You were never supposed to love me. I wasn’t prepared for it … <br />I always knew I would fall in love with you … but you were never supposed to love me back.”</i><br /><br />…and then this…<br /><br /><i>“I never stopped loving you. Not for one second.”</i><br /><br />WAAAAAAAAIL!!! All of this, for me, played out to a song that is mentioned in the book, which I had playing on repeat during the last part of the book and it just turned me into a gibbering mess! And just when I calmed myself down, there is a beautiful epilogue which set me off again. <br /><br />I absolutely adored these characters! They are both so real! Michael is a flawed guy, with a traumatic background who had a rough time growing up but has made a good life for himself. He has an absolutely adorable 3 year old daughter, and when he sees Lauren again he wants so badly to make amends for the past and have her back in his life. And Lauren is a wonderful heroine! She’s so genuine. Strong, smart, funny and confident, she goes through a lot in this book, but she’s always honest with herself and what she’s feeling and I completely understood her thought processes and actions. Love her!<br /><br />Shout out to Adam, I loved his addition to the cast. He’s absolutely gorgeous and pretty much perfect boyfriend material. The love triangle element is definitely there, with the chemistry definitely there between Lauren and Adam, but it’s more about what these two guys represent in her life – perfect vs flawed, and part of Lauren's struggle is to work through who she should want and who actually has her heart.<br /><br />I cannot gush enough about this book and how much I loved it. It’s a superbly written, intensely emotional read with humour, drama, and some gorgeously swoony moments (both romantic swoon, and platonic swoon - God I wish I had a friend like Michael when I was a teenager!!!). It astounds me that this is the author’s first novel! I will definitely be keeping an eye out for more of Priscilla Glenn’s work. <br /><br />EVERYBODY, EVERYWHERE – READ THIS BOOK AND READ IT NOW!!!!!<br /><br />6 sensationally shining stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4331339195026233995" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_455502642" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/455502642" />
    <a title="Richa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2796667-richa"><img alt="Richa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1354430575p2/2796667.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/455502642?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Richa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Richa" href="/user/show/2796667-richa">Richa</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/447172965" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/447172965?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer447172965" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8184175891536094218"><i>Back to You</i> is a sweet and endearing read about love lost and second chances. It eloquently portrays the bonds of true love and what one is willing to endure all in the name of love. <br/><br/>The book begins in present time where we meet Lauren, a  childcare worker who has been hurt in the past by her high school best friend and first love—Michael Delaney. This story is told in third person, as it weaves in and out of the past, slowly revealing Michael's betrayal. I enjoyed the slight aspect of suspense </span>
  <span id="freeText8184175891536094218" style="display:none"><i>Back to You</i> is a sweet and endearing read about love lost and second chances. It eloquently portrays the bonds of true love and what one is willing to endure all in the name of love. <br><br>The book begins in present time where we meet Lauren, a  childcare worker who has been hurt in the past by her high school best friend and first love—Michael Delaney. This story is told in third person, as it weaves in and out of the past, slowly revealing Michael's betrayal. I enjoyed the slight aspect of suspense created in the process. <br><br>Lauren was quite possibly the most kindhearted, generous heroine I've ever had the pleasure of reading about. There were times where she came across as overly meek and I found myself mentally persuading her to stand up for herself...but her unconditional love and unique ability to understand all was both humbling and inspiring. <br><br>Michael Delaney, aka 'Del', with his mysterious countenance and intriguing, wounded persona captures Lauren's interest at first sight back in high school. He has endured a traumatic past that has left him detached and guarded--but Lauren attempts to break down those barriers as they form a shaky but an ultimately unbreakable bond. <br><br>Priscilla Glenn's writing was flawless and took me on a truly heartwarming journey. There was another love interest incorporated, but this story did not snowball into a love triangle. If you're looking for an amazing and touching tale about broken hearts redeemed—this is your book! <br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_446445556" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/446445556" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz"><img alt="Elizabeth (Liz)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551206872p2/5495317.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/446445556?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=ebook-read">ebook-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=contemporary-romance-read">contemporary-romance-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=arc-from-author-read">arc-from-author-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer446445556" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6140187781545364514">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><br/>4 1/2 Stars! Priscilla Glenn's Back To You is a wonderfully romantic story from a fantastic debut author!!<br/><br/>Lauren Monroe and Michael Delaney met in high school. She was an incoming freshman, and he was a sophomore. She got good grades, participated in gymnastics and did what was expected of her. He could have cared less about studying, participated in nothing but having a good time and was often suspended from school for one violation or another. She was a g</span>
  <span id="freeText6140187781545364514" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><br />4 1/2 Stars! Priscilla Glenn's Back To You is a wonderfully romantic story from a fantastic debut author!!<br /><br />Lauren Monroe and Michael Delaney met in high school. She was an incoming freshman, and he was a sophomore. She got good grades, participated in gymnastics and did what was expected of her. He could have cared less about studying, participated in nothing but having a good time and was often suspended from school for one violation or another. She was a good girl. He was a bad boy. There should have been no foundation from which a friendship could grow, and, yet, that's exactly what happened. Somehow, during those following three years, Lauren Monroe and Michael Delaney became best friends. Best friends who, eventually, began to straddle the line into something more. Best friends who wound up separated from each other for years due to personal demons.<br /><br />It's now eight years later, and there have been inevitable changes in both of their lives. When they meet again, it's a shock, and their shared past begins to slowly replay, over time, in both of their heads. Have they changed enough to be able to finally make a future together, or have they changed too much?<br /><br /><br /><br />For me, Back To You is the best of both worlds. The story opens in present day, and is told through a series of flashbacks to Lauren's and Michael's high school years alternating with their lives intersecting again in the present. <br /><br />Over time, I have become more and more enamored with YA/New Adult romance. I've been reading so many of those, in fact, that it has become almost exclusively so in the last month or two. So, when I first learned Back To You is categorized as adult contemporary romance, I realized I was going to have to leave my current comfort zone of YA/New Adult. I wasn't sure I was ready to do that. Thankfully, because of the way this story is written, there is nearly an entire YA book within its pages. One of my very favorite things about Back To You is the fact that I was able to relive Lauren and Michael's high school relationship with them. Their history is integral to the story, to any possible future they may have, and it is told so well by Priscilla Glenn. I see a complete YA/New Adult romance in your future, Ms. Glenn (or, maybe that's just my fervent wish)! <br /><br />What I almost didn't expect to happen, was to rediscover my love for adult contemporary romance through the reading of this book. But, that's *precisely* what happened. The characters' interactions in the present day became just as compelling as reading about their young-adult relationship. It was interesting to see how they had changed and grown....and how they hadn't. It was fascinating to have all of their history right there, to be allowed to experience their past, and to watch them interact again in the present as adults. That adult relationship, reconnection, was made so much richer and fuller for the way the story as a whole was written. This richness, this fullness, is what is all too often lacking from contemporary romances today. <br /><br />Back To You is a well-written story of young love and second chances. It's sweet, romantic, real, and has just enough angst to make you truly feel and root for the characters and their future. As an added bonus, there is a touching and simply wonderful epilogue, for which I thank the author very much.<br /><br />Priscilla Glenn, you have a new fan, and I am so looking forward to more from you!!<br /><br /><br /><br />*A copy was kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review*<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6140187781545364514" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781479103782" href="/book/show/16114910-back-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454487003" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9183393169351864905"><b>
  <i>”That thing that made her heart come alive in her chest and her body thrum with emotion and her soul felt like it was home. Right back to him, always to him.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>This is a really beautiful story about true once in a lifetime love, friendship and second chances. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>”Well, sometimes if something is really important to you, it gets stuck in your body. So even if your mind things that it’s gone, it’s still there, kind of hiding inside of you, just waiting for you to remember. It never goes away.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>W</span>
  <span id="freeText9183393169351864905" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”That thing that made her heart come alive in her chest and her body thrum with emotion and her soul felt like it was home. Right back to him, always to him.” </i>
</b><br /><br />This is a really beautiful story about true once in a lifetime love, friendship and second chances. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>”Well, sometimes if something is really important to you, it gets stuck in your body. So even if your mind things that it’s gone, it’s still there, kind of hiding inside of you, just waiting for you to remember. It never goes away.”</b>
</i><br /><br />When sweet good girl Lauren Monroe met the high school’s bad boy Michael Delaney ‘Del’ the unlikely duo become best friends all through high school. Michael has a crappy home life and many issues with the loss of his brother. Lauren is one of the only people he truly lets in. She gets to see a whole different side of Michael then the rest of the school. After Michael graduates high school and is getting ready to move to New York, their relationship gets complicated...<br /><br /><b>
  <i>”For as long as I’ve know you, you’ve given me a part of you that you haven’t given anyone else. And now I’m finally getting to do the same.”</i>
</b><i></i><br /><br /> After one night together, Michael moves to NY and doesn’t really speak or contact Lauren again... fast forward 8 years... Lauren gets a new job teaching at a daycare while going back to school to get her masters. None other than Michael shows up on her first day with his daughter Erin(who I absolutely adore!) At first, Lauren doesn’t know how to act around Michael. She tries to be professional with him, but its hard and the lines of friendship/professionalism blur. How do you act around your former best friend, and first/only real love? <br /><br />Lauren... I loved her. What strong and sweet mc. She was really wonderful. I loved how she just <i>got</i> Michael. She was able to move past all the hurt and forgive. <br /><b>
  <i>”It was about redemption. Everyone deserved the chance to be redeemed.”</i>
</b><br />Michael, Michael, Michael... How could you not fall in love with this guy? Everything he did, he did because he truly though it was the best thing for those he loved. Seeing him with his daughter just made my love for him even stronger. He was wonderful!<br /><br /><i>
  <b> “I always knew I would fall in love with you,” he said softly, “but you were never supposed to love me back.”</b>
</i><br /><br />This book made my heart melt at times, and broke my heart at times. By the end, I had the hugest smile on my face! I want more of Lauren and Michael! Read read read!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="9183393169351864905" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer464005096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer620791958616097135">I don't think I have words to describe how AMAZING this book is. I'm absolutely floored by this book it had emotion pouring out of it by the bucket load, I know that I am going to sound overboard but I just can't help it, I loved every chapter, Micheal and Lauren have got to be my most favourite characters, if you have not read this book READ IT. Two love stories in one compelling, heart wrenching book that you will not be able to put down and one that will stay will you long after the final pag</span>
  <span id="freeText620791958616097135" style="display:none">I don't think I have words to describe how AMAZING this book is. I'm absolutely floored by this book it had emotion pouring out of it by the bucket load, I know that I am going to sound overboard but I just can't help it, I loved every chapter, Micheal and Lauren have got to be my most favourite characters, if you have not read this book READ IT. Two love stories in one compelling, heart wrenching book that you will not be able to put down and one that will stay will you long after the final page. *sigh*<br /><br />I Started this book before around a month ago and found it difficult to get into but after seeing such great reviews decided to give it ago again, sometimes it isn't the book but yourself that stops you from enjoying a book. This was all on me and how wrong was I. The second time around i started it and barely put it down untill i finished it I was so addicted to this book I LOVED it.<br /><br />The author cleverly introduces us to the main characters by switching between present day and the past by ordering the chapters by months &amp; years, I loved this way of bringing the reader right into the story it made me feel I was living the story (I sound dramatic I know) this book had me well and truly hooked.<br /><br />Straight away I knew I would like micheal delaney 'del' who can resist a tortured hero? The author weaves information to the reader in an addictive manner, willing the reader to find out more.<br />Laurens character is built up more slowly from the start not quite your A typical shy student, she shows strength from the get go.<br /><br />The connection between del and Lauren is toe curling my heart was lost in their romance from the beginning.<br /><br />"she was one of the most genuine people he'd ever met, and he knew at that moment that I'd he did nothing else in his life, he wanted to be friends with Lauren Monroe."<br /><br />"she couldn't help but smile at the irony of the fact that the baddest boy in school could somehow always make her feel like the world was good."<br /><br />This book is so heart wrenching I cried laughed and felt the whole way through. The book left me so full of emotion, I just want to read it all again. I can't express what a special and endearing story this is. The author has done an amazing job of making a story so alive, it feels like an honour to have read such a heart warming epic romance. If I could give this book ten stars I would. From start to finish I adored this book.</span>

<div id="review_453582926" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/453582926" />
    <a title="Sara " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5058304-sara"><img alt="Sara " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1439650883p2/5058304.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/453582926?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara " href="/user/show/5058304-sara">Sara </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=debut-read-from-new-to-me-author">debut-read-from-new-to-me-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=can-t-miss-book">can-t-miss-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=a-must-read">a-must-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453582926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6475110557110816094">What a wonderful debut from Priscilla Glenn! To say I liked this book would be an understatement! I <b>LOVED</b> this book! I could not put it down. I don’t stay up until 2am reading because I like the look of luggage under my eyes!<br/><br/>This is a beautifully told friends to lover’s story with a twist. The story is told with dual perspectives and alternating time lines and I love the way this story was written. The writing is gorgeous; it is flawless and seamless in its transition from past to present to giv</span>
  <span id="freeText6475110557110816094" style="display:none">What a wonderful debut from Priscilla Glenn! To say I liked this book would be an understatement! I <b>LOVED</b> this book! I could not put it down. I don’t stay up until 2am reading because I like the look of luggage under my eyes!<br /><br />This is a beautifully told friends to lover’s story with a twist. The story is told with dual perspectives and alternating time lines and I love the way this story was written. The writing is gorgeous; it is flawless and seamless in its transition from past to present to give you the story of this unrequited, unsung and undeniable love.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Well, sometimes if something is really important to you, it gets stuck in your body. So even if your mind thinks that it’s gone, it’s still there, kind of hiding inside of you, just waiting for you to remember. It never goes away."</i>
</b><br /><br />Lauren Monroe is starting a new job teaching at a day care facility while goes back to school. On her first day as she is welcoming a new student she is shocked by who she sees standing with the little girl. Someone from her past she never thought she would see again.<br /><br />Michael Delany is suddenly thrown into her Lauren’s life; it has been eight years without contact from him. Lauren is hurt, she is angry and she is confused. Her friend, her best friend who disappeared from her life was suddenly back. At this moment I knew this book would be different. I felt Lauren’s reaction to Michael. I wasn’t told how to feel, the words flew off the page and resonated within my emotions. I was hooked and ready to jump aboard the Michael and Lauren train. I needed to know what happened in their past, and I needed to know what would happen to them now.<br /><br />Lauren met Michael in high school; these two on the surface seem so different but there is something that draws Lauren to Michael. After an outburst in class she begins to wonder who this “bad boy” is that everyone is so afraid of. She decides to ignore the rumors and gets to see the real person behind the label.<br /><br />Michael has a past that had led him to be a boy who loses control. His reputation follows him around school but the day that Lauren takes a chance on him is the day that will change him forever.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"It was about redemption. Everyone deserved a chance to be redeemed."</i>
</b><br /><br />The complicated relationship between Lauren and Michael is beautiful. These young friends lean on each other for support, comfort and encouragement. They are there when no one else can be or wants to be. The understanding they have goes beyond the definition of friendship to what one could call a soul mate. The line of friendship begins to blur when emotions are confronted, confused and contrite.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"She couldn’t help but smile at the irony that the baddest boy in school could somehow always make her feel like the world was good. And when he winked at her, she knew beyond a shadow of a doubt that from that moment on, she would do anything for him."</i>
</b> <br /><br />Through the telling of their story you are engrained in their lives. You are there with each and every monumental moment that will lead them to where they are now. Michael’s past is heartbreaking. I cannot believe the guilt he holds onto and has burdened himself with from such a young age. It has made Michael into the boy we first meet and ultimately the man he turns out to be.<br /><br />Lauren is a strong woman who has tried to move passed the hurt. She has tried to move on without closure of what happened between her and Michael eight years ago. It isn’t the easiest thing to do when you still ask yourself why and the one who holds the answers is right in front of you daily. I waited and held my breath to see who would make the first move.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"He’d spent eight years missing her, but this time it was different. He couldn’t help but ask himself the question; if he could go back and do it all differently, would he?"</i>
</b> <br /><br />Oh that first move and all that happened in between! Sigh. I loved Jenn, she was such a good friend to Lauren from the beginning. Adam, oh sweet and handsome Adam! He was necessary to Lauren’s growth and I will never get the image of him in that apron during the cooking class out my head.<br /><br />I cannot say enough how much I fell in love with this story. There is no overt sexuality beating you over the head yet you feel the tension between Lauren and Michael. There is no filler, no fluff there is just amazing words that fit together perfectly to grip you by the heart and not let you go. I cannot stop thinking about Dirty Dancing, silver leaves, dinner plates, foam pits and what to really do when life gives you lemons!<br /><br />Back to you is a wonderful story about the strength of love; strength to give your love, to hold onto love and hold out for that love. It is a story about hope, survival, forgiveness and redemption.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"That thing that made her heart come alive in her chest and her body thrum with emotion and her soul felt like it was home. Right back to him, always to him."</i>
</b> <br /><br /><i>Review copy provided by the Author. Thank You! </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6475110557110816094" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer456508529" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6312314182020511285"><br/>You can also find this review at <a href='http://prufreads.blogspot.in/2012/12/guest-review-by-fathima.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Texxie's blog </a> !!!! She was kind enough to have me as her guest reviewer !! * Happy dance *<br/><br/><b>
  <i> “Well, sometimes if something is really important to you, it gets stuck in your body,” he said, poking her ribs and making her laugh. “So even if your mind thinks that it’s gone, it’s still in there, kind of hiding inside of you, just waiting for you to remember. It never goes away.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>Michael Michael Michael .... <br/><br/><a href='http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&current=hugs.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397730ra/767681.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Boy , you made me cry .. <br/><br/><b> * sigh * </b><br/><br/>I'm a huge sucker</span>
  <span id="freeText6312314182020511285" style="display:none"><br>You can also find this review at <a href="http://prufreads.blogspot.in/2012/12/guest-review-by-fathima.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Texxie's blog </a> !!!! She was kind enough to have me as her guest reviewer !! * Happy dance *<br><br><b>
  <i> “Well, sometimes if something is really important to you, it gets stuck in your body,” he said, poking her ribs and making her laugh. “So even if your mind thinks that it’s gone, it’s still in there, kind of hiding inside of you, just waiting for you to remember. It never goes away.” </i>
</b><br><br>Michael Michael Michael .... <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=hugs.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397730ra/767681.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Boy , you made me cry .. <br><br><b> * sigh * </b><br><br>I'm a huge sucker for 'second chance' romances and the question I asked myself after reading this book was , ' Why the hell didn't I read this sooner ??!!! ' .. Sooo absolutely good . See the thing here is that , the same concept or the same story can be told many times but what makes it stand out is the way the author chooses to tell the story . In short , the story telling ability of the author can give the same old story of 'girl-meeting-boy-then-boy-leaving-girl-only-to-come-back-after-a-period-of-time' a new breath of life . And that's exactly what Priscilla Glenn does with <b> Back to you </b> .<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=walkaway-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397730i/767682.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lauren Monroe teaches and takes care of kids at Learn and Grow Day Care . She is a very kind , very lovable kind of a person . Optimistic and assuring , she always manages to see and bring out the best in people . But one fine day , she comes face to face with a face from her past . A face that mirrors and harbors a lot of emotions and feeling within her . The face of Michael Delaney . Michael Delaney is a changed man . A man who always used to let his fist do the talking somehow managed to keep his demons under control because of a friendship he shared with a very special girl .. A girl who saw the human in him and not the monster . But then one day he broke her heart . How , why , when , where .... ? Those are questions you need to tackle on your own ... I'm just gonna leave this bit here with this :<br><br><a href="http://www.cherrybam.com/love-quotes.php" title="Love Quotes, Love Quotes Images, Love Sayings" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/298703.gif" alt="Love Quotes, Love Quotes Images, Love Sayings" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The story is beautifully woven ... <br><br>I cried <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=tears.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397730i/767683.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I laughed<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=laughingemoticon.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397730i/767684.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I smiled <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=kitty-smile.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397730i/767685.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I swooned <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=17_swooningoverheart.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397730i/767686._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The journey that was Michael and Lauren's relationship was just breath taking ! I loved Priscilla Glenn story telling ... I loved how the story moved back and forth from the present to the past . Everything felt the same yet felt different . The first time Lauren met Michael in the past , her feelings were those of intrigue and curiousity . But when she meets him again in the present , her feelings are that of being surprised , a little anger , a little disappointment and a whole lot of confusion ... What I really enjoyed about it as a whole was that , it kind of seemed that history was repeating itself , by bringing these two face to face again , but this time it only took a different route with different obstacles to cross . They had each other then , they have each other now . Will the same mistakes be repeated , or will they finally be together .. Read the book and find out !!! <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/holding%20hands/pixelett/holding_hands-620x320-1.jpg?o=8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397730i/767687._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One of my fav characters other than Michael and Lauren was Erin , Michael's daughter ! Sometimes kids I tell ya , they act way more mature than adults do ! And she definitely was the mature one here ! I loved Michael and Erin's relationship . I loved how he wanted to be the world for Erin . A.M.A.Z.I.N.G !!! <br><br>If you love a story that makes you cry sweet , happy and sad tears at the same time , then Back to you is just for you !!!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="6312314182020511285" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_454675661" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454675661" />
    <a title="Leanne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9138991-leanne"><img alt="Leanne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1335687728p2/9138991.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454675661?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leanne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leanne" href="/user/show/9138991-leanne">Leanne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454675661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6706240891786522887"> <b>Books like this, which read so beautifully and flawlessly, remind me on every single page why I fell in love with reading.</b><br/><br/>I absolutely did not want this book to end. I kept trying to prolong the experience, to savor every single word on every single page, but I suppose you can only delay the inevitable for so long.<br/><br/>This book pulled me in immediately, with exceptionally written scenes and lovable characters. I can honestly say I fell madly in love with every single character in this book. One of </span>
  <span id="freeText6706240891786522887" style="display:none"> <b>Books like this, which read so beautifully and flawlessly, remind me on every single page why I fell in love with reading.</b><br /><br />I absolutely did not want this book to end. I kept trying to prolong the experience, to savor every single word on every single page, but I suppose you can only delay the inevitable for so long.<br /><br />This book pulled me in immediately, with exceptionally written scenes and lovable characters. I can honestly say I fell madly in love with every single character in this book. One of the things which struck me was how much I loved both Adam and Michael. And one of the amazing things about this book was the way in which the author doesn’t make you like one of the prospective suitors less in order to fall in love with the hero. I love that “the other guy” wasn’t given some flaw or made to act in such a way to sway the reader in the other direction. I was able to fall in love with them both, yet at the same time be completely in sync with the progression and outcome of the story. <br /><br />Michael’s backstory absolutely broke my heart. The flashbacks to his past causing a tightening in my chest and an overwhelming desire to climb into those pages, pick up that little boy and envelop him in a tight embrace.<br /><br /><b>“But what if you forget you love me, like daddy did?” Michael said through his tears, and Aaron shook his head. “Never, I’ll never forget”.</b><br /><br />But seeing the man Michael had become- no longer a broken adolescent with a hair-trigger temper- and witnessing his interactions with his daughter, was a truly beautiful thing. Lauren was loving, loyal and caring, her nature, much like Michael’s, evident in her interactions with Erin, and I adored her as a heroine.<br /><br />The scenes felt so extraordinarily real that the simplest gesture could have my heart rate increasing and my nerves tingling. My emotions were so entangled in the story that a kiss made my heart swell, had my pulse racing and left me with goose bumps on my skin and butterflies in my stomach. The scenes were not about the mechanics behind them but the feeling and emotion captured in every movement, in every gesture.<br /><br />To put it simply, this book was a pleasure to read. I fell in love with the writing, with the story and with the characters and was saddened to read that final page, knowing the experience had come to an end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6706240891786522887" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_454067460" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454067460" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454067460?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781479103782" href="/book/show/16114910-back-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454067460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15262957638446726023">If you are in mood for strongly <b>emotioanl</b> story, go for this one. This is definitely one of the most emotional stories I have ever read - it made me smile, it made me cry and I even had goose bumps couple of times. Back To You is beautifully written book and I highly recommend it!!!<br/><br/>This story has its cute moments, sad moments, moments full of love and moments full of heartbreak. Basically, it has everything that really good contemporary novel should have. Moreover, I love stories where we get ch</span>
  <span id="freeText15262957638446726023" style="display:none">If you are in mood for strongly <b>emotioanl</b> story, go for this one. This is definitely one of the most emotional stories I have ever read - it made me smile, it made me cry and I even had goose bumps couple of times. Back To You is beautifully written book and I highly recommend it!!!<br /><br />This story has its cute moments, sad moments, moments full of love and moments full of heartbreak. Basically, it has everything that really good contemporary novel should have. Moreover, I love stories where we get chapters from present as well as from past. There is not many of them out there and it makes them pretty special, and Back To You is VERY special. <br /><br /><b>Lauren</b><br />Lauren was incredibly sweet person. She was caring, forgiving and lovely. I could see it as well as all characters in this book could too.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>"I think she's really a princess, but she just forgets to wear her crown."</b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Michael</b><br />Everyone perceived Michael Devlon as dangerous person, but Lauren was drawn to him from very beginning, mainly beause she saw something different and worthy behind his facade. Michael maybe had difficult childhood and it made him angry but never a bad person. My heart broke for him so many times during this book. It was so sad to read about young boy going through hard emotional times when nothing was his fault...<br /><blockquote>
  <b>"He was too lovely to be menacing but too intense to be innocent."</b>
</blockquote><br />I liked the fact that Michael liked Lauren not only because she treated him differently than other poeple. There was real affection and love between them, not something superficial. Moreover, proces of falling in love between Lauren and Michael was absolutely believable. These days, there are plenty of novels where characters fall in love immediately without enough explanation why or how. Fortunatelly, it was not the case with this book. So go and read it, you won't regret it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15262957638446726023" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
